# Results of the 2013 Malaysian state elections by constituency

*Source: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Results_of_the_2013_Malaysian_state_elections_by_constituency*

---

{{Short description|none}}
[[File:Dewan_Undangan_Negeri_2013_Equal_Area.svg|thumb|400px|Equal-area representation of the results with each hexagon representing one seat]]
These are the '''election results of the [[2013 Malaysian general election]] by state constituency'''. [[State legislative assemblies of Malaysia|State assembly]] elections were held in [[Malaysia]] on 5 May 2013 as part of the general elections. These [[Malaysian State Assembly Representatives (2013–)|members of the legislative assembly]] (MLAs) representing their constituency from the first sitting of respective state legislative assembly to its dissolution.<ref>Election Results of the 13th Malaysian General Elections {{cite web |url=http://keputusan.spr.gov.my/ |title=Dashboard PRU13 |access-date=2013-04-23 |url-status=dead |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20130423092454/http://keputusan.spr.gov.my/ |archive-date=2013-04-23 }}</ref><ref>Star Online Election Results http://elections.thestar.com.my/results/results.aspx {{Webarchive|url=https://web.archive.org/web/20150228075224/http://elections.thestar.com.my/results/results.aspx |date=2015-02-28 }}</ref><ref>Sabah Parliament&mdash;Official Results at a Glance http://borneoinsider.com/sabah-parliament-official-results-at-a-glance/ {{Webarchive|url=https://web.archive.org/web/20130508143233/http://borneoinsider.com/sabah-parliament-official-results-at-a-glance/ |date=2013-05-08 }}</ref><ref>New Straits Times Election Results http://www.nst.com.my/ge13</ref>

The state legislature election deposit was set at [[Malaysian ringgit|RM]] 5,000 per candidate. Similar to previous elections, the election deposit will be forfeited if the particular candidate had failed to secure at least 12.5% or one-eighth of the votes.
